  1027:   function aicmOrgShowUpdateConfirm(payload) {
  1028:     state.pendingOrgUpdate = payload || null;
  1029:     var root = document.getElementById("aicm-root");
  1030:     if (!root) {
  1031:       setMessage("error", "確認画面を表示できません。");

  1037: 
  1038:   async function executeAicmOrgUpdateConfirm() {
  1039:     var payload = state.pendingOrgUpdate || null;
  1040: 
  1041:     if (!payload || !payload.endpoint || !payload.body) {
  1042:       setMessage("error", "確認対象がありません。");
  1043:       return;
  1044:     }
  1045: 
  1046:     try {
  1047:       await aicmOrgPostJson(payload.endpoint, payload.body);
  1048:             // AICM_AXC_EXECUTE_ROLE_PLACEMENT_SYNC_AFTER_MAIN_UPDATE

  5080: function aicmRenderManagerMajorRows(rows) {
  5081:     var sourceRows = Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [];
  5082:     var pendingRows = sourceRows.filter(function (row) {
  5083:       // AICM_R8Z_V9D1_IS_PENDING_MAJOR_SCOPE_CALLSITE_FIX: use existing visible canonical helper, not the scope-local isPendingMajor
  5084:       if (typeof aicmIsPendingManagerMajorRowR8V6 === "function") {
  5085:         return aicmIsPendingManagerMajorRowR8V6(row);
  5086:       }
  5087:       return !!row;
  5088:     });
  5089: 
  5090:     var confirmCard = aicmRenderMajorItemDeleteConfirmCardR8P();
  5091:

  5093:       return [
  5094:         confirmCard,
  5095:         '<div class="aicm-core-empty">',
  5096:         '  <strong>登録済み大項目はまだありません</strong>',
  5097:         '  <p>CSV取り込み後、未実行/未引き継ぎのManager大項目だけが表示されます。</p>',
  5098:         '</div>'
  5099:       ].join("");
  5100:     }
  5101: 
  5102:     var pageSize = aicmMajorItemPageSizeR8O();
  5103:     var totalRows = pendingRows.length;
  5104:     var totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(totalRows / pageSize));
  5105:     var page = aicmMajorItemCurrentPageR8O(totalRows);
  5106:     var start = (page - 1) * pageSize;
  5107:     var pageRows = pendingRows.slice(start, start + pageSize);
  5108: 
  5109:     var pager = [
  5110:       '<div class="aicm-dashboard-action-row">',
  5111:       '  <button type="button" data-core-action="pmlw-major-page-prev"' + (page <= 1 ? ' disabled' : '') + '>前ページ</button>',
  5112:       '  <span class="aicm-selected-note">ページ ' + escapeHtml(String(page)) + ' / ' + escapeHtml(String(totalPages)) + '　表示 ' + escapeHtml(String(start + 1)) + '-' + escapeHtml(String(start + pageRows.length)) + ' / ' + escapeHtml(String(totalRows)) + '件</span>',
  5113:       '  <button type="button" data-core-action="pmlw-major-page-next"' + (page >= totalPages ? ' disabled' : '') + '>次ページ</button>',
  5114:       '</div>'
  5115:     ].join("");
  5116: 
  5117:     var cards = pageRows.map(function (row, index) {

  5119:       var summary = aicmMajorItemSummaryR8O(row);
  5120:       var displayNo = start + index + 1;
  5121:

  5123:         '<article class="aicm-core-card aicm-major-item-row">',

  5125:         '  <h3>' + escapeHtml(summary.title) + '</h3>',
